\\tnflog NotificationLog\\n612: \\trecv  *nflogpb.Receiver\\n613: \\n614: \\tnow  func() time.Time\\n615: \\thash func(*types.Alert) uint64\\n616: }\\n617: \\n618: // NewDedupStage wraps a DedupStage {\\n669: \\t// If we haven't notified about the alert group before, notify right away\\n670: \\t// unless we only have resolved alerts.\\n671: \\tif entry == nil {\\n672: \\t\\treturn len(firing) > 0, has passed.\\n695: \\treturn entry.Timestamp.Before(n.now().Add(-repeat)), \\\"repeat\\\"\\n696: }\\n697: \\n698: // Exec implements the Stage interface.\\n699: func (n *DedupStage) Exec(ctx \\\"reason\\\", reason)\\n763: \\treturn ctx, alerts, nil\\n764: }\\n765: \\n766: // RetryStage notifies via passed integration with exponential backoff until it\\n767: // succeeds. \\treturn &MuteStage{muter: m, metrics: metrics}\\n549: }\\n550: \\n551: // Exec implements the Stage interface.\\n552: func (n *MuteStage) Exec(ctx context.Context, logger log.Logger, alerts \\tnflog NotificationLog\\n612: \\trecv  *nflogpb.Receiver\\n613: \\n614: \\tnow  func() time.Time\\n615: \\thash func(*types.Alert) uint64\\n616: }\\n617: \\n618: // NewDedupStage wraps a DedupStage '\\\\xff'\\n644: \\n645: \\thb := hashBuffers.Get().(*hashBuffer)\\n646: \\tdefer hashBuffers.Put(hb)\\n647: \\tb := hb.buf[:0]\\n648: \\n649: \\tnames := make(model.LabelNames, 0, xxhash.Sum64(b)\\n664: \\n665: \\treturn hash\\n666: }\\n667: \\n668: func (n *DedupStage) needsUpdate(entry *nflogpb.Entry, firing, resolved map[uint64]struct{}, repeat time.Duration) (bool, string) {\\n669: \\t// If we haven't notified about the alert group before, notify right away\\n670: \\t// unless we only have resolved alerts.\\n671: \\tif entry == nil {\\n672: \\t\\treturn len(firing) > 0, \\\"fire\\\"\\n673: \\t}\\n674: \\n675: \\tif !entry.IsFiringSubset(firing) {\\n676: \\t\\treturn true, \\\"fire subset\\\"\\n677: \\t}\\n678: \\n679: \\t// Notify about all alerts being has passed.\\n695: \\treturn entry.Timestamp.Before(n.now().Add(-repeat)), \\\"repeat\\\"\\n696: }\\n697: \\n698: // Exec implements the Stage interface.\\n699: func (n *DedupStage) Exec(ctx context.Context, l log.Logger, alerts ...*types.Alert) (context.Context, []*types.Alert, error) {\\n700: \\tgkey, ok := GroupKey(ctx)\\n701: \\tif !ok {\\n702: \\t\\treturn ctx, nil, \\tdefault:\\n746: \\t\\treturn ctx, nil, fmt.Errorf(\\\"unexpected entry result size %d\\\", len(entries))\\n747: \\t}\\n748: \\n749: \\tneedsUpdate, reason := n.needsUpdate(entry, firingSet, by other Alertmanager instance while this one was sleeping in WaitStage.\\n757: \\t\\t// In this case, this instance cannot proceed with the pipeline anymore because there is a risk that the instance holds the obsolete alerts, and it could cause flapping or duplicated notifications.\\n758: \\t\\t// This could happen only in high-availability mode.\\n759: \\t\\t_ = level.Warn(l).Log(\\\"msg\\\", \\\"Timestamp of notification log entry is after the current pipeline timestamp.\\\", \\\"entry_time\\\", entry.Timestamp, \\\"pipeline_time\\\", timeNow, \\\"diff\\\", diff, \\\"aggrGroup\\\", gkey, \\\"alerts\\\", fmt.Sprintf(\\\"%+v\\\", alerts), \\\"receiver\\\", n.recv.GroupName, \\\"integration\\\", n.recv.Integration, \\\"needsUpdateReason\\\", reason)\\n760: \\t\\treturn ctx, nil, \\\"reason\\\", reason)\\n763: \\treturn ctx, alerts, nil\\n764: }\\n765: \\n766: // RetryStage notifies via passed integration with exponential backoff until it\\n767: // succeeds. It aborts if the context is canceled or timed out.\\n768: type RetryStage struct {\\n769: \\tintegration *Integration\\n770: \\tgroupName   string\\n771: \\tmetrics     *Metrics\\n772: \\tlabelValues []string\\n773: }\\n774: \\n775: // NewRetryStage returns a new instance of a RetryStage.\\n776: func NewRetryStage(i *Integration, groupName string, metrics *Metrics) *RetryStage {\\n777: \\tr.metrics.numNotifications.WithLabelValues(r.labelValues...).Inc()\\n793: \\tctx, alerts, err := r.exec(ctx, l, alerts...)\\n794: \\n795: \\tfailureReason := DefaultReason.String()\\n796: \\tif err {\\n849: \\t\\tcase <-ctx.Done():\\n850: \\t\\t\\tif iErr == nil {\\n851: \\t\\t\\t\\tiErr = ctx.Err()\\n852: \\t\\t\\t\\tif errors.Is(iErr, context.Canceled) {\\n853: \\t\\t\\t\\t\\tiErr = \\t\\t\\tr.metrics.numNotificationRequestsTotal.WithLabelValues(r.labelValues...).Inc()\\n874: \\n875: \\t\\t\\tif err != nil {\\n876: \\t\\t\\t\\tr.metrics.numNotificationRequestsFailedTotal.WithLabelValues(r.labelValues...).Inc()\\n877: \\t\\t\\t\\tif !retry {\\n878: \\t\\t\\t\\t\\treturn ctx, alerts, fmt.Errorf(\\\"%s/%s: notify \\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\tlevel.Warn(l).Log(\\\"msg\\\", \\\"Notify attempt failed, will retry later\\\", \\\"attempts\\\", i, \\\"err\\\", err)\\n884: \\t\\t\\t\\t\\t}\\n885: \\t\\t\\t\\t\\t// Save this {\n430: \tvar fs FanoutStage\n431: \tfor i := range integrations {\n432: \t\trecv := &nflogpb.Receiver{\n433: \t\t\tGroupName:   name,\n434: \t\t\tIntegration: integrations[i].Name(),\n435: \t\t\tIdx: \treturn fs\n446: }\n447: \n448: // RoutingStage executes the inner stages based on the receiver specified in\n449: // the context.\n450: type RoutingStage map[string]Stage\n451: \n452: // Exec fail.\n491: func (fs FanoutStage) Exec(ctx context.Context, l log.Logger, alerts ...*types.Alert) (context.Context, []*types.Alert, error) {\n492: \tvar (\n493: \t\twg sync.WaitGroup\n494: \t\tme alerts, nil\n512: }\n513: \n514: // GossipSettleStage waits until the Gossip has settled to forward alerts.\n515: type GossipSettleStage struct {\n516: \tpeer Peer\n517: }\n518: \n519: // )\n539: \n540: // MuteStage filters alerts through a Muter.\n541: type MuteStage struct {\n542: \tmuter   types.Muter\n543: \tmetrics *Metrics\n544: }\n545: \n546: // NewMuteStage return a new ctx.Err()\n603: \t}\n604: \treturn ctx, alerts, nil\n605: }\n606: \n607: // DedupStage filters alerts.\n608: // Filtering happens based on a notification log.\n609: type DedupStage struct {\n610: \trs    ResolvedSender\n611: \tnflog NotificationLog\n612: \trecv  *nflogpb.Receiver\n613: \n614: \tnow  func() time.Time\n615: \thash func(*types.Alert) uint64\n616: }\n617: \n618: // NewDedupStage wraps a DedupStage that runs against the given notification log.\n619: func NewDedupStage(rs ResolvedSender, l NotificationLog, recv *nflogpb.Receiver) *DedupStage {\n620: \treturn &DedupStage{\n621: \t\trs:    rs,\n622: \t\tnflog: l,\n623: \t\trecv:  recv,\n624: \t\tnow:   utcNow,\n625: \t\thash:  hashAlert,\n626: \t}\n627: }\n628: \n629: func utcNow() time.Time {\n630: \treturn time.Now().UTC()\n631: }\n632: \n633: // Wrap a slice in a struct so we can store a pointer in sync.Pool.\n634: type hashBuffer struct {\n635: \tbuf []byte\n636: }\n637: \n638: var hashBuffers = sync.Pool{\n639: \tNew: func() interface{} { return &hashBuffer{buf: make([]byte, 0, 1024)} },\n640: }\n641: \n642: func hashAlert(a *types.Alert) uint64 {\n643: \tconst sep = '\\xff'\n644: \n645: \thb := hashBuffers.Get().(*hashBuffer)\n646: \tdefer hashBuffers.Put(hb)\n647: \tb := hb.buf[:0]\n648: \n649: \tnames := make(model.LabelNames, 0, len(a.Labels))\n650: \n651: \tfor ln := range a.Labels {\n652: \t\tnames = append(names, ln)\n653: \t}\n654: \tsort.Sort(names)\n655: \n656: \tfor _, ln := range names {\n657: \t\tb = append(b, string(ln)...)\n658: \t\tb = append(b, sep)\n659: \t\tb = append(b, string(a.Labels[ln])...)\n660: \t\tb = append(b, sep)\n661: \t}\n662: \n663: \thash := xxhash.Sum64(b)\n664: \n665: \treturn hash\n666: }\n667: \n668: func (n *DedupStage) needsUpdate(entry *nflogpb.Entry, firing, resolved map[uint64]struct{}, repeat time.Duration) (bool, string) {\n669: \t// If we haven't notified about the alert group before, notify right away\n670: \t// unless we only have resolved alerts.\n671: \tif entry == nil {\n672: \t\treturn len(firing) > 0, \"fire\"\n673: \t}\n674: \n675: \tif !entry.IsFiringSubset(firing) {\n676: \t\treturn true, \"fire subset\"\n677: \t}\n678: \n679: \t// Notify about all alerts being resolved.\n680: \t// This is done irrespective of the send_resolved flag to make sure that\n681: \t// the firing alerts are cleared from the notification log.\n682: \tif len(firing) == 0 {\n683: \t\t// If the current alert group and last notification contain no firing\n684: \t\t// alert, it means that some alerts have been fired and resolved during the\n685: \t\t// last interval. In this case, there is no need to notify the receiver\n686: \t\t// since it doesn't know about them.\n687: \t\treturn len(entry.FiringAlerts) > 0, \"resolve\"\n688: \t}\n689: \n690: \tif n.rs.SendResolved() && !entry.IsResolvedSubset(resolved) {\n691: \t\treturn true, \"resolve subset\"\n692: \t}\n693: \n694: \t// Nothing changed, only notify if the repeat interval has passed.\n695: \treturn entry.Timestamp.Before(n.now().Add(-repeat)), \"repeat\"\n696: }\n697: \n698: // Exec implements the Stage interface.\n699: func (n *DedupStage) Exec(ctx context.Context, l log.Logger, alerts ...*types.Alert) (context.Context, []*types.Alert, error) {\n700: \tgkey, ok := GroupKey(ctx)\n701: \tif !ok {\n702: \t\treturn ctx, nil, errors.New(\"group key missing\")\n703: \t}\n704: \n705: \trepeatInterval, ok := RepeatInterval(ctx)\n706: \tif !ok {\n707: \t\treturn ctx, nil, errors.New(\"repeat interval missing\")\n708: \t}\n709: \n710: \ttimeNow, ok := Now(ctx)\n711: \tif !ok {\n712: \t\treturn ctx, alerts, errors.New(\"missing now timestamp\")\n713: \t}\n714: \n715: \tfiringSet := map[uint64]struct{}{}\n716: \tresolvedSet := map[uint64]struct{}{}\n717: \tfiring := []uint64{}\n718: \tresolved := []uint64{}\n719: \n720: \tvar hash uint64\n721: \tfor _, a := range alerts {\n722: \t\thash = n.hash(a)\n723: \t\tif a.Resolved() {\n724: \t\t\tresolved = append(resolved, hash)\n725: \t\t\tresolvedSet[hash] = struct{}{}\n726: \t\t} else {\n727: \t\t\tfiring = append(firing, hash)\n728: \t\t\tfiringSet[hash] = struct{}{}\n729: \t\t}\n730: \t}\n731: \n732: \tctx = WithFiringAlerts(ctx, firing)\n733: \tctx = WithResolvedAlerts(ctx, resolved)\n734: \n735: \tentries, err := n.nflog.Query(nflog.QGroupKey(gkey), nflog.QReceiver(n.recv))\n736: \tif err != nil && !errors.Is(err, nflog.ErrNotFound) {\n737: \t\treturn ctx, nil, err\n738: \t}\n739: \n740: \tvar entry *nflogpb.Entry\n741: \tswitch len(entries) {\n742: \tcase 0:\n743: \tcase 1:\n744: \t\tentry = entries[0]\n745: \tdefault:\n746: \t\treturn ctx, nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected entry result size %d\", len(entries))\n747: \t}\n748: \n749: \tneedsUpdate, reason := n.needsUpdate(entry, firingSet, resolvedSet, repeatInterval)\n750: \tif !needsUpdate {\n751: \t\treturn ctx, nil, nil\n752: \t}\n753: \t// now make sure that the current state is from past\n754: \tif entry != nil && entry.Timestamp.After(timeNow) {\n755: \t\tdiff := entry.Timestamp.Sub(timeNow)\n756: \t\t// when entry's timestamp is greater than the flushing time, it means that the pipeline was already ran by other Alertmanager instance while this one was sleeping in WaitStage.\n757: \t\t// In this case, this instance cannot proceed with the pipeline anymore because there is a risk that the instance holds the obsolete alerts, and it could cause flapping or duplicated notifications.\n758: \t\t// This could happen only in high-availability mode.\n759: \t\t_ = level.Warn(l).Log(\"msg\", \"Timestamp of notification log entry is after the current pipeline timestamp.\", \"entry_time\", entry.Timestamp, \"pipeline_time\", timeNow, \"diff\", diff, \"aggrGroup\", gkey, \"alerts\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%+v\", alerts), \"receiver\", n.recv.GroupName, \"integration\", n.recv.Integration, \"needsUpdateReason\", reason)\n760: \t\treturn ctx, nil, nil\n761: \t}\n762: \t_ = level.Debug(l).Log(\"msg\", \"Need to notify\", \"aggrGroup\", gkey, \"receiver\", n.recv.GroupName, \"integration\", n.recv.Integration, \"reason\", reason)\n763: \treturn ctx, alerts, nil\n764: }\n765: \n766: // RetryStage notifies via passed integration with exponential backoff until it\n767: // succeeds. It aborts if the context is canceled or timed out.\n768: type RetryStage struct {\n769: \tintegration *Integration\n770: \tgroupName   string\n771: \tmetrics     *Metrics\n772: \tlabelValues []string\n773: }\n774: \n775: // NewRetryStage returns a new instance of a RetryStage.\n776: func NewRetryStage(i *Integration, groupName string, metrics *Metrics) *RetryStage {\n777: \tlabelValues := []string{i.Name()}\n778: \n779: \tif metrics.ff.EnableReceiverNamesInMetrics() {\n780: \t\tlabelValues = append(labelValues, i.receiverName)\n781: \t}\n782: \n783: \treturn &RetryStage{\n784: \t\tintegration: i,\n785: \t\tgroupName:   groupName,\n786: \t\tmetrics:     metrics,\n787: \t\tlabelValues: labelValues,\n788: \t}\n789: }\n790: \n791: func (r RetryStage) Exec(ctx context.Context, l log.Logger, alerts ...*types.Alert) (context.Context, []*types.Alert, error) {\n792: \tr.metrics.numNotifications.WithLabelValues(r.labelValues...).Inc()\n793: \tctx, alerts, err := r.exec(ctx, l, alerts...)\n794: \n795: \tfailureReason := DefaultReason.String()\n796: \tif err != nil {\n797: \t\tvar e *ErrorWithReason\n798: \t\tif errors.As(err, &e) {\n799: \t\t\tfailureReason = e.Reason.String()\n800: \t\t}\n801: \t\tr.metrics.numTotalFailedNotifications.WithLabelValues(append(r.labelValues, failureReason)...).Inc()\n802: \t}\n803: \treturn ctx, alerts, err\n804: }\n805: \n806: func (r RetryStage) exec(ctx context.Context, l log.Logger, alerts ...*types.Alert) (context.Context, []*types.Alert, error) {\n807: \tvar sent []*types.Alert\n808: \n809: \t// If we shouldn't send notifications for resolved alerts, but there are only\n810: \t// resolved alerts, report them all as successfully notified (we still want the\n811: \t// notification log to log them for the next run of DedupStage).\n812: \tif !r.integration.SendResolved() {\n813: \t\tfiring, ok := FiringAlerts(ctx)\n814: \t\tif !ok {\n815: \t\t\treturn ctx, nil, errors.New(\"firing alerts missing\")\n816: \t\t}\n817: \t\tif len(firing) == 0 {\n818: \t\t\treturn ctx, alerts, nil\n819: \t\t}\n820: \t\tfor _, a := range alerts {\n821: \t\t\tif a.Status() != model.AlertResolved {\n822: \t\t\t\tsent = append(sent, a)\n823: \t\t\t}\n824: \t\t}\n825: \t} else {\n826: \t\tsent = alerts\n827: \t}\n828: \n829: \tb := backoff.NewExponentialBackOff()\n830: \tb.MaxElapsedTime = 0 // Always retry.\n831: \n832: \ttick := backoff.NewTicker(b)\n833: \tdefer tick.Stop()\n834: \n835: \tvar (\n836: \t\ti    = 0\n837: \t\tiErr error\n838: \t)\n839: \n840: \tl = log.With(l, \"receiver\", r.groupName, \"integration\", r.integration.String())\n841: \tif groupKey, ok := GroupKey(ctx); ok {\n842: \t\tl = log.With(l, \"aggrGroup\", groupKey)\n843: \t}\n844: \n845: \tfor {\n846: \t\ti++\n847: \t\t// Always check the context first to not notify again.\n848: \t\tselect {\n849: \t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n850: \t\t\tif iErr == nil {\n851: \t\t\t\tiErr = ctx.Err()\n852: \t\t\t\tif errors.Is(iErr, context.Canceled) {\n853: \t\t\t\t\tiErr = NewErrorWithReason(ContextCanceledReason, iErr)\n854: \t\t\t\t} else if errors.Is(iErr, context.DeadlineExceeded) {\n855: \t\t\t\t\tiErr = NewErrorWithReason(ContextDeadlineExceededReason, iErr)\n856: \t\t\t\t}\n857: \t\t\t}\n858: \n859: \t\t\tif iErr != nil {\n860: \t\t\t\treturn ctx, nil, fmt.Errorf(\"%s/%s: notify retry canceled after %d attempts: %w\", r.groupName, r.integration.String(), i, iErr)\n861: \t\t\t}\n862: \t\t\treturn ctx, nil, nil\n863: \t\tdefault:\n864: \t\t}\n865: \n866: \t\tselect {\n867: \t\tcase <-tick.C:\n868: \t\t\tnow := time.Now()\n869: \t\t\tretry, err := r.integration.Notify(ctx, sent...)\n870: \n871: \t\t\tduration := time.Since(now)\n872: \t\t\tr.metrics.notificationLatencySeconds.WithLabelValues(r.labelValues...).Observe(duration.Seconds())\n873: \t\t\tr.metrics.numNotificationRequestsTotal.WithLabelValues(r.labelValues...).Inc()\n874: \n875: \t\t\tif err != nil {\n876: \t\t\t\tr.metrics.numNotificationRequestsFailedTotal.WithLabelValues(r.labelValues...).Inc()\n877: \t\t\t\tif !retry {\n878: \t\t\t\t\treturn ctx, alerts, fmt.Errorf(\"%s/%s: notify retry canceled due to unrecoverable error after %d attempts: %w\", r.groupName, r.integration.String(), i, err)\n879: \t\t\t\t}\n880: \t\t\t\tif ctx.Err() == nil {\n881: \t\t\t\t\tif iErr == nil || err.Error() != iErr.Error() {\n882: \t\t\t\t\t\t// Log the error if the context isn't done and the error isn't the same as before.\n883: \t\t\t\t\t\tlevel.Warn(l).Log(\"msg\", \"Notify attempt failed, will retry later\", \"attempts\", i, \"err\", err)\n884: \t\t\t\t\t}\n885: \t\t\t\t\t// Save this error to be able to return the last seen error by an\n886: \t\t\t\t\t// integration upon context timeout.\n887: \t\t\t\t\tiErr = err\n888: \t\t\t\t}\n889: \t\t\t} else {\n890: \t\t\t\tlvl := level.Info(l)\n891: \t\t\t\tif i <= 1 {\n892: \t\t\t\t\tlvl = level.Debug(log.With(l, \"alerts\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", alerts)))\n893: \t\t\t\t}\n894: \n895: \t\t\t\tlvl.Log(\"msg\", \"Notify success\", \"attempts\", i, \"duration\", duration)\n896: \t\t\t\treturn ctx, alerts, nil\n897: \t\t\t}\n898: \t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n899: \t\t\tif iErr == nil {\n900: \t\t\t\tiErr = ctx.Err()\n901: \t\t\t\tif errors.Is(iErr, context.Canceled) {\n902: \t\t\t\t\tiErr = NewErrorWithReason(ContextCanceledReason, iErr)\n903: \t\t\t\t} else if errors.Is(iErr, context.DeadlineExceeded) {\n904: \t\t\t\t\tiErr = NewErrorWithReason(ContextDeadlineExceededReason, iErr)\n905: \t\t\t\t}\n906: \t\t\t}\n907: \t\t\tif iErr != nil {\n908: \t\t\t\treturn ctx, nil, fmt.Errorf(\"%s/%s: notify retry canceled after %d attempts: %w\", r.groupName, r.integration.String(), i, iErr)\n909: \t\t\t}\n910: \t\t\treturn ctx, nil, nil\n911: \t\t}\n912: \t}\n913: }\n914: \n915: // SetNotifiesStage sets the notification information about passed alerts. The\n916: // passed alerts should have already been sent to the receivers.\n917: type SetNotifiesStage struct {\n918: \tnflog NotificationLog\n919: \trecv  *nflogpb.Receiver\n920: }\n921: \n922: // NewSetNotifiesStage returns a new instance of a SetNotifiesStage.\n923: func NewSetNotifiesStage(l NotificationLog, recv *nflogpb.Receiver) *SetNotifiesStage {\n924: \treturn &SetNotifiesStage{\n925: time.\n969: func (tms TimeMuteStage) Exec(ctx context.Context, l log.Logger, alerts ...*types.Alert) (context.Context, []*types.Alert, error) {\n970: \tmuteTimeIntervalNames, ok := MuteTimeIntervalNames(ctx)\n971: \tif !ok {\n972: \t\treturn ctx, alerts, nil\n973: \t}\n974: \tnow, ok := Now(ctx)\n975: \tif !ok {\n976: \t\treturn ctx, alerts, errors.New(\"missing now
